      <div class="annotation_label">
        
          <h3 class="u-inline">
            About “Don't Wanna Know”
          </h3>
        
        
      </div>
      <div class="rich_text_formatting">
        <p>“Don’t Wanna Know” is a song about past lovers. Adam focuses on not wanting to know what his ex-lover has been up to or who she’s been with since they broke up, while Kendrick shows his ex what she’s been missing.</p>

<p>This is Maroon 5’s first single since 2015’s <a href="https://genius.com/Maroon-5-this-summers-gonna-hurt-like-a-motherfucker-lyrics" data-api_path="/songs/1862772">“This Summer’s Gonna Hurt Like A Motherfucker”</a> off of the rerelease of their fifth album, <a href="https://genius.com/albums/Maroon-5/V" data-api_path="/albums/105603"><em>V.</em></a></p>
      </div>
      <div class="song_metadata u-xx_large_bottom_margin"></div>
    </div>

    <div class="column_layout-column_span-initial_content">
      <div initial-content-for="question_list">
  <ul>
    
      <li  class="question question--bottom_border ">
  <div class="u-bottom_margin">
    <h3 class="annotation_label">Have Maroon 5 and Kendrick Lamar collaborated before?</h3>
  </div>
  
  <div class="rich_text_formatting rich_text_formatting--no_vertical_margins">
    <p>Maroon 5 and Kendrick have never collaborated previous to “Don’t Wanna Know,” however, Adam Levine and Kendrick were both featured artists on The Lonely Island’s <a href="https://genius.com/The-lonely-island-yolo-lyrics" data-api_path="/songs/112469">“YOLO.”</a></p>
  </div>


</li>

    
      <li  class="question question--bottom_border ">
  <div class="u-bottom_margin">
    <h3 class="annotation_label">Did Maroon 5 tease "Don't Wanna Know" leading up to the official release?</h3>
  </div>
  
  <div class="rich_text_formatting rich_text_formatting--no_vertical_margins">
    <p>Maroon 5 debuted a solo version of “Don’t Wanna Know” during September 3, 2016, at their live performance at the AT&amp;T Centre in San Antonio.</p>

      <li  class="question question--bottom_border ">
  <div class="u-bottom_margin">
    <h3 class="annotation_label">Does Kendrick collaborate with pop stars often?</h3>
  </div>
  
  <div class="rich_text_formatting rich_text_formatting--no_vertical_margins">
    <p>In fact, he does. He’s collaborated with <a href="https://genius.com/artists/Taylor-swift" data-api_path="/artists/1177">Taylor Swift</a> on <a href="https://genius.com/Taylor-swift-bad-blood-remix-lyrics" data-api_path="/songs/1866151">“Bad Blood (Remix),”</a> <a href="https://genius.com/artists/Beyonce" data-api_path="/artists/498">Beyoncé</a>’s <a href="https://genius.com/Beyonce-freedom-lyrics" data-api_path="/songs/2461233">“Freedom”</a> and <a href="https://genius.com/artists/Sia" data-api_path="/artists/16775">Sia’s</a> <a href="https://genius.com/Sia-the-greatest-lyrics" data-api_path="/songs/2849661">“The Greatest”</a> from 2015 to 2016. He’s also collaborated with <a href="https://genius.com/Imagine-dragons-radioactive-remix-lyrics" data-api_path="/songs/348633">Imagine Dragons,</a> <a href="https://genius.com/The-lonely-island-yolo-lyrics" data-api_path="/songs/112469">The Lonely Island</a> and <a href="https://genius.com/Awolnation-sail-tde-remix-lyrics" data-api_path="/songs/132580">AWOLNATION,</a> among others.</p>
  </div>


</li>

    
      <li  class="question question--bottom_border ">
